  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c6adff67-e721-4436-9f5e-1b4febc65842'

  <span id="freeText16288391919001476030" style="display:none">Tessa Gray thought her journey to London would be the beginning of a new life, but she never could have envisioned the dark turn that life would take... Abducted upon arrival, Tessa is introduced to London's Downworld, the sordid supernatural underbelly of the city, and informed that her future will be recast to service a man known as "The Magister". Only the intervention of the London Institute's Shadowhunters delivers the girl from this fate, but sinister forces are still gathering around Tessa. Even so, Tessa's attraction to two of the young Shadowhunters who have taken her under their wings may prove more dangerous by far...</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6360255225969614326">I decided to read the manga of Clockwork Angel, instead of re-reading the novel (mostly for the sake of saving myself a bit of time) before continuing on with the series.<br/>I really enjoyed Clockwork Angel, but I didn't really like it in this format at all. There was so much left out, which is understandable considering the different form. Unfortunately because of this it left me quite confused at times, as well as rather irritated with the characters and the rate at which some things occur was por</span>
  <span id="freeText6360255225969614326" style="display:none">I decided to read the manga of Clockwork Angel, instead of re-reading the novel (mostly for the sake of saving myself a bit of time) before continuing on with the series.<br />I really enjoyed Clockwork Angel, but I didn't really like it in this format at all. There was so much left out, which is understandable considering the different form. Unfortunately because of this it left me quite confused at times, as well as rather irritated with the characters and the rate at which some things occur was portrayed as just unrealistically fast.<br />I will definitely be continuing with the series (of novels.. I doubt I'll pick up the manga's for the rest of the books to read later on), don't get me wrong! I remember LOVING Clockwork Angel the first time I read it. It works so much better as a novel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6360255225969614326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2885958817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5559307011970651764">I am a most enthusiastic fan of Cassandra Clare, so yes yes I needed to try the graphic novel editions of The Infernal Devices! I also opened this book and realised several things: (1) I read Clockwork Angel in 2015 and remember nothinggggggg, (2) what was Tessa's power?, (3) I really missed this whole world. except for Will. What if Will went and ate a duck and didn't come back is all I'm saying. He's so very dramatic once you know his secret.<br/><br/>Anyway. Notable moments in this are:<br/>➢ The art was su</span>
  <span id="freeText5559307011970651764" style="display:none">I am a most enthusiastic fan of Cassandra Clare, so yes yes I needed to try the graphic novel editions of The Infernal Devices! I also opened this book and realised several things: (1) I read Clockwork Angel in 2015 and remember nothinggggggg, (2) what was Tessa's power?, (3) I really missed this whole world. except for Will. What if Will went and ate a duck and didn't come back is all I'm saying. He's so very dramatic once you know his secret.<br /><br />Anyway. Notable moments in this are:<br />➢ The art was super cute and I actually liked Tessa MORE in this than the prose book, because she had expressions. And she got so pissed off at Will. I stan.<br />➢ Magnus appeared with long flowing hair, gorgeous face, a floral suit, and I basically screamed. I love Magnus.<br />➢ I forgot how hilariously horrible Jessamine is.<br /><br />Basically Jessamine:<br /><blockquote>Jessamine: omg your brother could marry me<br />Tessa: he's unconscious right now???<br />Jessamine: [sniffs] I can still plan things<br />Tessa: hE IS GRAVELY ILL???????<br />Jessamine: is that a problem for our marriage </blockquote><br /><br />➢ Also all Shadowhunters are very racist towards anyone who isn't a Shadowhunter 🤔Not new. Just so much more obvious rereading these.<br />➢ I FORGOT Will said he's marrying the cook because "beauty doesn't last bUT COOKING IS ETERNAL". Lmao. The only time I liked him.<br />➢ Just look. See, look. Why would you care about Will when ✨Jem✨ is there being sweet and playing a violin and occasionally coughing up blood on the street while the girls save him.<br />➢ Also CHARLOTTE IS A GIFT.<br />➢ Ok I really want to reread the prose version now.<br /><br /><br />And apart from just loving the series in general (I like TMI better though and TDA most of all): my only things with the graphic novel were it skipped forward in scenes really fast. Sometimes it was confusing to realise we'd shifted POV/scene because it would happen from one panel to the next without a break. Jem did N O T get enough page time. But so freaking love how much more epic Tessa felt visually.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5559307011970651764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I highly recommend. :)</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9610623344297299533">Anyone who knows me knows that The Infernal Devices is my all time favorite series. I've been wanting to reread the series for months, but I have been busy trying to get through other books, so I have been putting it off. I recently got the graphic novels from the library to try to placate me in the meantime, and so far, I'm happy I did!<br/><br/>I really enjoyed this first installment of the graphic novels. It was cute, and I think the characters were pretty much on point with the novels. It was a quick </span>
  <span id="freeText9610623344297299533" style="display:none">Anyone who knows me knows that The Infernal Devices is my all time favorite series. I've been wanting to reread the series for months, but I have been busy trying to get through other books, so I have been putting it off. I recently got the graphic novels from the library to try to placate me in the meantime, and so far, I'm happy I did!<br /><br />I really enjoyed this first installment of the graphic novels. It was cute, and I think the characters were pretty much on point with the novels. It was a quick read, and it was fun, and it did exactly as I intended - just something that I could read in the meantime until I had the time to sit down and reread the full novels. As this is a different medium than a traditional novel, things had to be cut out, so the story seemed to fly by. In some ways, this was good, but in others, it just made me want more. I am very excited for my reread of the actual book that will hopefully come in the next month or so!<br /><br />If you are a fan of The Infernal Devices, I recommend this book because it was cute and did a good job portraying the events of Clockwork Angel.</span>

  <span id="freeText12148847735461568412" style="display:none">*** <b>Warning: this review contains scans</b> ***<br><br>Truth, I love manga but hate books adaptation into graphic novels. I had read The Infernal Device series in the original novel form and loved it. But to be able to get a visual of everything going on is just great. I wanted to read the manga adaption for a while but I couldn't find the 3rd book so I put it on hold, but ri</span>
  <span id="freeText14946375797645945554" style="display:none"><i>I try to express only my most honest opinion in a spoiler-free way. Unfortunately, there is still always a risk of slight spoilers despite my best efforts. If you feel something in my review is a spoiler please let me know. Thank you.</i><br /><br />Loved it. I had read The Infernal Device series in the original novel form and loved it. But to be able to get a visual of everything going on is just great. I wanted to read the manga adaption for a while but I couldn't find the 3rd book so I put it on hold, but right now all 3 books are on Kindle Unlimited. YAY! So I finally get to read this series. I admit that the appearance of the characters are different than I imagined, but this is a manga and they have a certain style. I will be reading the next in series soon.</span>

<div id="review_1812312319" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1812312319" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52343138-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604747861p2/52343138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1812312319?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/52343138-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52343138-lauren?shelf=manga">manga</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1812312319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11298396192575659021">*big sigh* Well, that was delicious!<br/><br/>I think having never read the novel has worked well for me here. I notice some GR users are disgruntled by the graphic novel version but since this is my first introduction to the Infernal Devices world, I have to say I bloody loved it! <br/><br/>The illustrations by Hyekyung Baek are absolutely stunning. I can see myself having a few of the them on my wall that's how beautiful they are. Plus, her chibi doodles are adorable! <br/><br/>Clockwork Angel is set in Victorian London wh</span>
  <span id="freeText11298396192575659021" style="display:none">*big sigh* Well, that was delicious!<br /><br />I think having never read the novel has worked well for me here. I notice some GR users are disgruntled by the graphic novel version but since this is my first introduction to the Infernal Devices world, I have to say I bloody loved it! <br /><br />The illustrations by Hyekyung Baek are absolutely stunning. I can see myself having a few of the them on my wall that's how beautiful they are. Plus, her chibi doodles are adorable! <br /><br />Clockwork Angel is set in Victorian London where we meet Tessa Gray, an American, who is taken under the Enclave's wings (headed by Charlotte and Henry Branwell), after Tessa is rescued by Will Herondale (who is quite beautiful) from the Dark Sisters and their evil employer, the Magister. (Yes, a lot of things do happen in this opening novel which makes it such compelling reading!)<br /><br />I'm not going to give much away in terms of the plot because it's a simply beautiful read; if you like a strong story told well, then Clockwork Angel is for you. There are vampires, shadowhunters, downworlders and of course, the Magister himself (which isn't who you expect it to be...well, I didn't think it was this character).<br /><br />And then we come to James (Jem) Carstairs who is my favourite character because he is just so beautiful. I mean, yes, Will is very attractive, but he knows it, and comes across as a little smug and conceited at times, but Jem (swoons) he is beautiful and doesn't make a deal out of it which is wonderful. Plus we learn something quite upsetting about his childhood which explains his current ghostly complexion :'( <br /><br />There is plenty of action along the way, plenty of exposition and a whole motley crew of beautiful and intriguing characters (Lady Belcourt and Magnus Bane to name two). <br /><br />I'd recommend this to people who like steampunk/Victorian fantasy stories and who appreciate high-quality manga. Go check it out! </span>
  <a data-text-id="11298396192575659021" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4428235-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360760658p2/4428235.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644788850?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/4428235-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Clockwork Angel and manga</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=angels-and-demons">angels-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=steampunk">steampunk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=manga">manga</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=laughed-out-loud">laughed-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4428235-anna?shelf=brotastic-bromance">brotastic-bromance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644788850" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7511999244372807321">Found it at my library and decided to skim through it.<br/><br/><u>
  <b>Pros:</b>
</u><br/><b>*</b> Followed the story well.<br/><br/><b>*</b> The art style is fairly shojo (which I don't personally prefer) but it's well done.<br/><br/><b>*</b> The characters designs are pretty accurate and rather cute.<br/><br/><b>*</b> There are a few scenes where the characters went "chibi" or had other humorous expressions famously used in manga. I found it both adorable and funny and it made it feel a little more "authentic" as a manga.<br/><br/><br/><u>
  <b>Cons:</b>
</u><br/><b>*</b> I know Henry was kind of a derpy character in</span>
  <span id="freeText7511999244372807321" style="display:none">Found it at my library and decided to skim through it.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Pros:</b>
</u><br /><b>*</b> Followed the story well.<br /><br /><b>*</b> The art style is fairly shojo (which I don't personally prefer) but it's well done.<br /><br /><b>*</b> The characters designs are pretty accurate and rather cute.<br /><br /><b>*</b> There are a few scenes where the characters went "chibi" or had other humorous expressions famously used in manga. I found it both adorable and funny and it made it feel a little more "authentic" as a manga.<br /><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Cons:</b>
</u><br /><b>*</b> I know Henry was kind of a derpy character in the books but come on! The poor guy doesn't even get a real face. He at least could've been given a face during the serious moments. <br /><br /><b>*</b> Remember that grotesque scar Sophie has? The one Clare describes as basically twisting the side of her face? It looks like a cat scratch in this book.<br /><br /><b>*</b> The best line in the <i>Clockwork Angel</i> - Magnus's <i>"Black hair and blue eyes are my favorite combination"</i> - is not to be found. It's just... not there.<br /><br /><b>*</b> I have a feeling not everyone will appreciate the "chibi" moments. Even though I thought it was cute at some points, it felt inappropriate at others. I think that's more about personal opinion though; it just wasn't how I would have visualized the scene.<br /><br /><br /><br />Overall it's neat for anyone who loves <i>Clockwork Angel</i>, loves manga, and loves seeing books visualized. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7511999244372807321" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1638675709" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1638675709" />
    <a title="Justine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7617291-justine"><img alt="Justine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557685507p2/7617291.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1638675709?book_show_action=true">May 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Justine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Justine" href="/user/show/7617291-justine">Justine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7617291-justine?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1638675709" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17392714395722140548">At first, it really felt like the manga had been made only for those who had read the original work. The first 70 pages were very confusing at times, it made the whole thing almost obnoxious. But once I got around to understand who everyone was and what everyone did, it became more interesting! However, I'm pretty sure there's a lot I'm still unaware of because of how much was cut from the book (which is understandable since the books are massive!).<br/><br/>Will Herondale is as annoying as Clary & Jace i</span>
  <span id="freeText17392714395722140548" style="display:none">At first, it really felt like the manga had been made only for those who had read the original work. The first 70 pages were very confusing at times, it made the whole thing almost obnoxious. But once I got around to understand who everyone was and what everyone did, it became more interesting! However, I'm pretty sure there's a lot I'm still unaware of because of how much was cut from the book (which is understandable since the books are massive!).<br /><br />Will Herondale is as annoying as Clary &amp; Jace in The Mortal Instruments, which makes the read unnecessarily painful. But I have hope he'll grow on me and it's quite nice to have so many other main characters to get on well with! <br /><br />And now I want to read the sequel or want the books, so I guess the manga did its job! :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="17392714395722140548" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1402309473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1402309473" />
    <a title="Melissa Chung" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17703155-melissa-chung"><img alt="Melissa Chung" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1427492410p2/17703155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1402309473?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa Chung" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa Chung" href="/user/show/17703155-melissa-chung">Melissa Chung</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1402309473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16436692763629756694">I loved this manga. I like that in manga's they show the emotions dramatically. That always cracks me up. Also that they find the funny lines from books if it is based on a book and really bring that to the front. <br/><br/>This manga stuck with the original very well and made me angry in all the same places. Not much else to say about this one. I loved the original and I really liked this one. Can't wait to get Clockwork Prince.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('y9Zwc9m24hbqKG3grzG0/8ebgyLSY1UyJiLfDKnXBoajA/kUHI4xzdjUqnjCx3doFdVCXzhA0K4iM5hx4AJhew==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RjzD+nD4D/E1U/OMyiVodR8UDXG9ynrm+yaa+po1+UIu6UqdtcDcKgevNBSn06vizVrMDFfp/3r/N92H0+Cevw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11329875788576676929">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br/><br/>"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilo</span>
  <span id="freeText11329875788576676929" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
